## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    Start[db_query_dict] --> Check{db_conn provided?}
    Check -->|No| GetConn[get_eta_db]
    Check -->|Yes| CreateCursor
    GetConn --> CreateCursor[Create DictCursor]
    CreateCursor --> Execute[Execute Query]
    Execute --> Error{Error?}
    Error -->|Interface/Operational Error| Recursive{Recursive Call?}
    Recursive -->|No| Retry[Reconnect and Retry]
    Retry --> CreateCursor
    Recursive -->|Yes| Raise[Raise Error]
    Error -->|No Error| Fetch[Fetch All Results]
    Fetch --> Convert[Convert to Dict List]
    Convert --> Close[Close Cursor]
    Close --> Return[Return Results]
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class DatabaseConnection {
        +get_eta_db(autocommit)
        +db_query_dict(query_str, db_conn, _recursive_call)
        +execute_query(query_str, db_conn)
    }
    class ModelTypeOperations {
        +get_model_types()
        +get_model_type_config(model_type_name, breakcache)
        +set_model_type_config(model_type_name, config_dict)
    }
    class MLAlgorithmOperations {
        +set_ml_algorithm_for_model_type(model_type_name, algorithm_id, db_conn)
        +add_algorithm(algorithm_dict, parent_algorithm_id, model_type_name, features, user_id)
        +get_algorithm(algorithm_id)
        +get_all_algorithm()
        +remove_algorithm(algorithm_id)
        +get_algorithm_for_model_type(model_type_name)
        +ml_algorithm_query(model_type_name, features_to_query, db_conn)
        +get_algorithm_for_model_type_and_generator(model_type_name, generator_algorithm_id, db_conn)
    }
    class UserAuthOperations {
        +create_user(email, password, firstname, lastname, is_admin)
        +get_user(email)
        +list_users()
        +delete_user(email, id)
        +set_password(email, password)
        +set_admin(email, is_admin)
        +check_authorization(email, password)
        +is_admin(email)
    }
    DatabaseConnection --> ModelTypeOperations
    DatabaseConnection --> MLAlgorithmOperations
    DatabaseConnection --> UserAuthOperations
```

## Diagram 5

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Client
    participant add_algorithm
    participant get_eta_db
    participant Database
    participant set_ml_algorithm

    Client->>add_algorithm: Call with params
    add_algorithm->>get_eta_db: Get connection
    get_eta_db->>Database: Connect
    Database-->>get_eta_db: Connection
    get_eta_db-->>add_algorithm: db_conn
    add_algorithm->>Database: INSERT INTO ml_algorithm
    Database-->>add_algorithm: Return algorithm_id
    alt model_type_name provided
        add_algorithm->>set_ml_algorithm: Link to model_type
        set_ml_algorithm->>Database: UPDATE model_type
        Database-->>set_ml_algorithm: Success
        set_ml_algorithm->>Database: Commit
        set_ml_algorithm-->>add_algorithm: Done
    else no model_type_name
        add_algorithm->>Database: Commit
    end
    add_algorithm-->>Client: Return algorithm_id
```

## Diagram 6

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> CheckConnection
    CheckConnection --> CreateConnection: No Connection
    CheckConnection --> ExecuteQuery: Has Connection
    CreateConnection --> GetEnvironment
    GetEnvironment --> GetSecrets
    GetSecrets --> ConnectDB
    ConnectDB --> SetAutocommit
    SetAutocommit --> ExecuteQuery
    ExecuteQuery --> CheckError
    CheckError --> RetryOnce: Connection Error & First Try
    CheckError --> FetchResults: Success
    CheckError --> RaiseError: Error & Retry Exhausted
    RetryOnce --> CreateConnection
    FetchResults --> ConvertToDict
    ConvertToDict --> CloseCursor
    CloseCursor --> [*]
    RaiseError --> [*]
```

## Diagram 7

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    A[User Request] --> B{Operation Type}
    B -->|Read| C[Model Type Queries]
    B -->|Read| D[Algorithm Queries]
    B -->|Read| E[User Queries]
    B -->|Write| F[Model Type Updates]
    B -->|Write| G[Algorithm Updates]
    B -->|Write| H[User Management]
    C --> I[get_eta_db]
    D --> I
    E --> I
    F --> I
    G --> I
    H --> I
    I --> J[(PostgreSQL Database)]
    J --> K[Return Results]
```
